# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c1b-102">Membros obsoletos no .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c1b-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="15c1b-103">As tabelas deste artigo listam os membros de tipo obsoletos no .NET Framework 4.5 e em versões posteriores, organizados por assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c1b-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c1b-104">Use os links a seguir para ver uma lista dos membros obsoletos e as alternativas recomendadas em cada assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c1b-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c1b-105">Este artigo não lista os membros de tipos obsoletos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c1b-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c1b-106">Para obter uma lista de tipos obsoletos, consulte [Tipos obsoletos](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c1b-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

## <a name="obsolete-members-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="15c1b-140">Membros obsoletos em assemblies de sistema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c1b-140">Obsolete Members in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="15c1b-141">As tabelas a seguir listam os membros obsoletos em assemblies de sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c1b-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="15c1b-142">Esses assemblies são usados no desenvolvimento de aplicativos de uso\-geral direcionados ao .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="15c1b-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
